The Miami details in this game are insane. As a local and lifelong Floridian Iâ€™m blown away by the accuracy.  The building on the far left at 2:17 is definitely the Loewâ€™s Hotel in present day South Beach.  The plane banner discussed at 2:43 is super accurate because E11even Nightclub in Downtown Miami really does promote their club on airplane banners at the beach.  The building at 3:10 is definitely the building at 500 Brickell Avenue Condominium in the Brickell neighborhood which is a high-end luxury condo neighborhood.  The arena off to the left at 5:05 is definitely the Kaseya Center which is the arena where the Miami Heat actively play in Downtown Miami, which can be seen as you head west back onto the mainland from Miami Beach back into Miami proper on your left-hand side as you drive on Interstate 395. Notice the Vice City pink and baby blue colors that the Heat actively use.  The art mural off to the far right at 5:52 is by a famous Miami artist by the name of AHOLSNIFFSGLUE who is a Miami staple whose art can be seen all over the city going back years and especially in Miamiâ€™s Wynwood art district neighborhood that is discussed at this point of the video.  You can absolutely tell that Rock Star really studied the neighborhoods that they chose to highlight and recreate in the game. A lot of these things will only be understood by locals or those who have frequented our city several times within the last 10 years.
